This enhances the security and control over file transfers in and outside of the network.\r\n\r\nTrial\r\nFTP Manager Pro provides a free 7-day trial. You can access all the features of the application during the trial period.  After the 7-day trial is completed, you will be charged the monthly fee to continue using FTP Manager Pro. To avoid any subscription fee, cancel the subscription during the trial period from the Microsoft Store.  Even after canceling you can still create and edit the connection profiles in FTP Manager Pro but you will not be able to transfer the files.  At any time you can choose a monthly or yearly subscription to re-enable all features.\r\n\r\nUse the power of FTP Manager Pro to transfer your files securely.
